    SELECT [p1].[ProjectId], [p1].[UserId], [p1].[Role], [a0].[Id], [a0].[AvatarUrl], [a0].[Company], [a0].[Country], [a0].[CreatedAt], [a0].[Email], [a0].[FirstName], [a0].[FullName], [a0].[LastLoginAt], [a0].[LastName], [a0].[PasswordHash], [a0].[Phone], [a0].[ResetToken], [a0].[ResetTokenExpiry], [a0].[Timezone]
    FROM [ProjectMembers] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [AppUsers] AS [a0] ON [p1].[UserId] = [a0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProjectId]
WHERE [p].[OwnerId] = @__userId_0 OR EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [ProjectMembers] AS [p0]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProjectId] AND [p0].[UserId] = @__userId_0)
ORDER BY [p].[CreatedAt] DESC, [p].[Id], [a].[Id], [t].[ProjectId], [t].[UserId]

    FROM [ProjectMembers] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [AppUsers] AS [a0] ON [p1].[UserId] = [a0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [p].[Id] = [t].[ProjectId]
WHERE [p].[OwnerId] = @__userId_0 OR EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [ProjectMembers] AS [p0]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProjectId] AND [p0].[UserId] = @__userId_0)
ORDER BY [p].[CreatedAt] DESC, [p].[Id], [a].[Id], [t].[ProjectId], [t].[UserId]

WHERE [t].[AssigneeId] IS NOT NULL AND [t].[DueDate] IS NOT NULL AND [t].[DueDate] < @__now_0 AND [t].[Status] <> N'Completed'

SELECT [r].[Id], [r].[CreatedAt], [r].[FireAt], [r].[FiredAt], [r].[HasFired], [r].[NotifyEmail], [r].[NotifyInApp], [r].[TaskId], [r].[UserId], [t].[Id], [t].[AssigneeId], [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[Description], [t].[DueDate], [t].[IsStarred], [t].[Priority], [t].[ProjectId], [t].[Status], [t].[Title], [a].[Id], [a].[AvatarUrl], [a].[Company], [a].[Country], [a].[CreatedAt], [a].[Email], [a].[FirstName], [a].[FullName], [a].[LastLoginAt], [a].[LastName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[Phone], [a].[ResetToken], [a].[ResetTokenExpiry], [a].[Timezone]
FROM [Reminders] AS [r]
INNER JOIN [TaskItems] AS [t] ON [r].[TaskId] = [t].[Id]
INNER JOIN [AppUsers] AS [a] ON [r].[UserId] = [a].[Id]
WHERE [r].[HasFired] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [r].[FireAt] <= @__upTo_0
ORDER BY [r].[FireAt]
